│  1 import smtplib                                                                                                           │

│ 11     """                                                                                                                  │
│ 12     Template 40: The Scribe Deployment Engine.                                                                           │

│ 15     """                                                                                                                  │
│ 16     def __init__(self, sender_email="admin@sovereignnexus.org", app_password=None):                                      │
│ 17         self.log = MasterLog()                                                                                           │
│ 18         self.sender_email = sender_email                                                                                 │
│ 19         self.app_password = app_password # Set this via environment variable or input                                    │
│ 20         self.smtp_server = "smtp.gmail.com"                                                                              │
│ 21         self.smtp_port = 465 # SSL                                                                                       │
│ 22         self.context = ssl.create_default_context()                                                                      │
│ 23                                                                                                                          │
│ 24     def send_outreach_emails(self, draft_dir="Outreach_Drafts"):                                                         │
│ 25         """                                                                                                              │
│ 26         Loops through all text files in the draft directory and sends them.                                              │
│ 27         """                                                                                                              │
│ 28         if not self.app_password:                                                                                        │
│ 29             self.log.warn("SCRIBE FAILED: No App Password provided.")                                                    │
│ 30             return False                                                                                                 │
│ 31                                                                                                                          │
│ 32         draft_files = [f for f in os.listdir(draft_dir) if f.endswith(".txt")]                                           │
│ 33         if not draft_files:                                                                                              │
│ 34             self.log.info("NO DRAFTS FOUND: Deployment skipped.")                                                        │
│ 35             return                                                                                                       │
│ 36                                                                                                                          │
│ 37         with smtplib.SMTP_SSL(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port, context=self.context) as server:                         │
│ 38             try:                                                                                                         │
│ 39                 server.login(self.sender_email, self.app_password)                                                       │
│ 40                 self.log.info(f"SCRIBE LOGIN SUCCESS: {self.sender_email}")                                              │
│ 41             except Exception as e:                                                                                       │
│ 42                 self.log.error(f"SCRIBE LOGIN FAILED: {str(e)}")                                                         │
│ 43                 return False                                                                                             │
│ 44                                                                                                                          │
│ 45             for draft_file in draft_files:                                                                               │
│ 46                 file_path = os.path.join(draft_dir, draft_file)                                                          │
│ 47                 with open(file_path, 'r') as f:                                                                          │
│ 48                     content = f.read()                                                                                   │
│ 49                                                                                                                          │
│ 50                 # Basic parsing: First line is Subject, rest is Body                                                     │
│ 51                 lines = content.splitlines()                                                                             │
│ 52                 subject = lines[0].replace("Subject: ", "")                                                              │
│ 53                 body = "                                                                                                 │
│ 54 ".join(lines[1:])                                                                                                        │
│ 55                                                                                                                          │
│ 56                 # Identify recipient from filename (mapping required in manifest)                                        │
│ 57                 # For this first strike, we'll need to pass the target email manually or from manifest.                  │
│ 58                 target_name = draft_file.replace(".txt", "").replace("_", " ").split(" 2026")[0]                         │
│ 59                 recipient_email = self._get_recipient_email(target_name)                                                 │
│ 60                                                                                                                          │
│ 61                 if not recipient_email:                                                                                  │
│ 62                     self.log.warn(f"RECIPIENT NOT FOUND: Skipping {target_name}")                                        │
│ 63                     continue                                                                                             │
│ 64                                                                                                                          │
│ 65                 msg = EmailMessage()                                                                                     │
│ 66                 msg.set_content(body)                                                                                    │
│ 67                 msg["Subject"] = subject                                                                                 │
│ 68                 msg["From"] = self.sender_email                                                                          │
│ 69                 msg["To"] = recipient_email                                                                              │
│ 70                                                                                                                          │
│ 71                 try:                                                                                                     │
│ 72                     server.send_message(msg)                                                                             │
│ 73                     self.log.info(f"STRIKE DEPLOYED: {target_name} at {recipient_email}")                                │
│ 74                     # Update Manifest (Simulated update)                                                                 │
│ 75                     self._mark_as_delivered(target_name)                                                                 │
│ 76                     # Fidelity Delay (Mimic human)                                                                       │
│ 77                     time.sleep(30)                                                                                       │
│ 78                 except Exception as e:                                                                                   │
│ 79                     self.log.error(f"DEPLOYMENT FAILED for {target_name}: {str(e)}")                                     │
│ 80                                                                                                                          │
│ 81         return True                                                                                                      │
│ 82                                                                                                                          │
│ 83     def _get_recipient_email(self, target_name):                                                                         │
│ 84         # Placeholder mapping for this session. In future, we'll pull from dominion_manifest.json                        │
│ 85         mapping = {                                                                                                      │
│ 86             "Unis Logistics": "info@unislogistics.com", # SIMULATED                                                      │
│ 87             "A2 Global Shipping LLC": "contact@a2global.com", # SIMULATED                                                │
│ 88             "Sumrell Sugg, P.A.": "partners@sumrellsugg.com", # SIMULATED                                                │
│ 89             "Michelle Jerome Law": "mjerome@vanceborolaw.com" # SIMULATED                                                │
│ 90         }                                                                                                                │
│ 91         return mapping.get(target_name)                                                                                  │
│ 92                                                                                                                          │
│ 93     def _mark_as_delivered(self, target_name):                                                                           │
│ 94         self.log.info(f"TRUTH REGISTERED: Outreach for {target_name} is marked as DELIVERED.")                           │
│ 95                                                                                                                          │
│ 96 if __name__ == "__main__":                                                                                               │

│ 98     print("ScribeSend Engine Loaded.")                                                                                   │
